<div style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;height:2pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border:0;margin:30pt 5.88% 30pt 5.88%;"></div><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:5.88%;padding-right:5.88%;position:relative;"><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><a id="_e04ce5fe_06c1_4085_9beb_c47d63aa02d7"></a><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Section&#160;2&#160;&#8211; Financial Information</b></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Item&#160;2.02 &#8211; Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">On July 26, 2023, O&#8217;Reilly Automotive,&#160;Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its 2023 second quarter earnings. &#160;The text of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99.2.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Section 5 &#8211; Corporate Governance and Management</b></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="font-weight:bold;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Item 5.02 &#8211; Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers</b></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="font-weight:bold;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">On July 26, 2023, the Company issued a press release announcing that Greg Johnson, the Company&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;), informed the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of his intention to retire from the Company effective January 31, 2024. &#160;The Board has selected Brad Beckham, the Company&#8217;s Co-President, to succeed Mr. Johnson as CEO upon Mr. Johnson&#8217;s retirement. &#160;The Board has also determined that Brent Kirby, the Company&#8217;s Co-President, will be promoted to President upon Mr. Johnson&#8217;s retirement.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Beckham, age 44, has been an O&#8217;Reilly Team Member since 1996. Mr. Beckham&#8217;s O&#8217;Reilly career began as a Parts Specialist and progressed through the roles of Store Manager, District Manager, Regional Manager, Divisional Vice President, Vice President of Eastern Store Operations and Sales, Senior Vice President of Eastern Store Operations and Sales, Senior Vice President of Central Store Operations and Sales, Executive Vice President of Store Operations and Sales, and Executive Vice President and Chief Operating Officer. &#160;Mr. Beckham has held the position of Co-President since January of 2023.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Kirby, age 55, has been an O&#8217;Reilly Team Member since 2018. &#160;Mr. Kirby began his 35 year retail career with Lowe&#8217;s Companies, Inc. (&#8220;Lowe&#8217;s&#8221;) as a hardware associate and progressed through various positions at the store, district, and regional levels before being promoted to Senior Vice President of Store Operations and later Chief Omnichannel Officer. &#160;Prior to joining O&#8217;Reilly, Mr. Kirby held the position of Chief Supply Chain Officer for Lowe&#8217;s. &#160;In 2018, Mr. Kirby&#8217;s O&#8217;Reilly career began as Senior Vice President of Omnichannel and progressed through the roles of Executive Vice President of Supply Chain and Executive Vice President and Chief Supply Chain Officer. &#160;Mr. Kirby has held the position of Co-President since January of 2023.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">The Human Capital and Compensation Committee of the Board (the &#8220;Compensation Committee&#8221;) recommended, and the Board approved, maintaining the current annual base salary and annual performance incentive compensation for Messrs. Johnson, Beckham, and Kirby at this time. &#160;The Compensation Committee will evaluate Messrs. Beckham&#8217;s and Kirby&#8217;s full compensation plan, including, but not limited to, base salary, cash-based incentive compensation, equity-based incentive compensation and other perquisites, at the time of Mr. Johnson&#8217;s retirement and Messrs. Beckham&#8217;s and Kirby&#8217;s promotions and will provide a recommendation to the Board at that time.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">There are no arrangements or understandings between Mr. Beckham or Mr. Kirby and any other person pursuant to which Mr. Beckham or Mr. Kirby was selected as an officer, there are no family relationships between Mr. Beckham or Mr. Kirby and any director or other officer of the Company, and there are no transactions in which the Company is a party and in which Mr. Beckham or Mr. Kirby has a material interest subject to disclosure under Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><span style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">The text of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:10pt;margin:0pt;"><span style="font-weight:bold;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</span></p><p style="font-family:'Times New style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) (</font><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Nasdaq: </font><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">ORLY), a leading retailer in the automotive aftermarket industry, today announced the Company&#8217;s leadership succession plan. &#160;Greg Johnson, the Company&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;), has informed the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors (the &#8220;Board&#8221;) of his intention to retire from the Company effective January 31, 2024. &#160;The Board has selected Brad Beckham, the Company&#8217;s Co-President, to succeed Mr. Johnson as CEO upon Mr. Johnson&#8217;s retirement. &#160;The Board has also determined that Brent Kirby, the Company&#8217;s Co-President, will be promoted to President upon Mr. Johnson&#8217;s retirement.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';line-height:1.28;margin-bottom:8pt;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">Executive Chairman of the Board, Greg Henslee, commented, &#8220;On behalf of the Board, I would like to express my sincere gratitude to Greg for his 41 years of dedicated service to O&#8217;Reilly and, most importantly, for his outstanding leadership as CEO during a truly momentous phase of our Company&#8217;s history. &#160;Greg has mentored and developed a strong executive leadership team who led the Company through a period of unprecedented growth, driving record profitability. &#160;Greg is extremely passionate about and committed to perpetuating the O&#8217;Reilly Culture and is relentlessly focused on driving excellent customer service in all aspects of our business. &#160;Above all, Greg has been a champion for O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s promote from within philosophy and our dedication to long-term succession planning, and he has done an exemplary job preparing both Brad Beckham and Brent Kirby for their new roles. &#160;Brad shares Greg&#8217;s passion for O&#8217;Reilly. &#160;He is a highly respected member of our executive team whose considerable experience and significant industry knowledge make him exceptionally qualified to succeed Greg as CEO. &#160;Brent is also a proven leader and his extensive retail supply chain and omnichannel experience is critical to successfully driving our Company&#8217;s strategic initiatives. &#160;The Company is well prepared for this executive leadership transition and the Board remains highly confident in Team O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s ability to continue to generate long-term value for our shareholders.&#8221;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';line-height:1.28;margin-bottom:8pt;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p such a privilege to play a part in O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s incredible growth story,&#8221; stated Mr. Johnson. &#160;&#8220;Without any doubt, our success and achievements have been driven by our dedicated Team Members who live our Culture values each day and consistently provide the highest level of service in our industry, and it has truly been an honor to work with this unbelievably talented team. &#160;During my tenure as CEO, Brad and Brent have both been critical members of the O&#8217;Reilly leadership team and their significant knowledge, combined with that of our entire experienced executive management team, positions the Company well to continue our record of 30 consecutive years of comparable store sales and operating income growth.&#8221;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New incredible honor to be chosen as the next CEO of our great Company. &#160;I am extremely humbled at the tremendous privilege it is to represent our over 88,000 dedicated and hardworking Team Members&#8221;, commented Mr. Beckham, who will become only the fourth CEO in O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s rich history. &#160;&#8220;When I joined Team O&#8217;Reilly as a parts professional in 1996, we focused on the fundamental concept of providing excellent customer service each and every day; 27 years later that principle is alive and well and remains the foundation for our continued success. &#160;David O&#8217;Reilly, Greg Henslee, and Greg Johnson have been great examples as leaders and, along with Brent and our entire leadership team, I am absolutely committed to perpetuating our Culture, expanding our market share, and driving profitable growth long into the future.&#8221;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">Mr. Kirby, age 55, has been an O&#8217;Reilly Team Member since 2018. &#160;Mr. Kirby began his 35 year retail career with Lowe&#8217;s Companies, Inc. (&#8220;Lowe&#8217;s&#8221;) as a hardware associate and progressed through various positions at the store, district, and regional levels before being promoted to Senior Vice President of Store Operations and later Chief Omnichannel Officer. &#160;Prior to joining O&#8217;Reilly, Mr. Kirby held the position of Chief Supply Chain Officer for Lowe&#8217;s. &#160;In 2018, Mr. Kirby&#8217;s O&#8217;Reilly career began as Senior Vice President of Omnichannel and progressed through the roles of Executive Vice President of Supply Chain and Executive Vice President and Chief Supply Chain Officer. &#160;Mr. Kirby has held the position of Co-President since January of 2023.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';line-height:1.28;margin-bottom:8pt;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. was founded in 1957 by the O&#8217;Reilly family and is one of the largest specialty retailers of automotive aftermarket parts, tools, supplies, equipment, and accessories in the United States, serving both the do-it-yourself and professional service provider markets. &#160;Visit the Company&#8217;s website at </font><u style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';"> for additional information about O&#8217;Reilly, including access to online shopping and current promotions, store locations, hours and services, employment opportunities, and other programs. &#160;As of June&#160;30,&#160;2023, the Company operated 6,071 stores across 48 U.S. states, Puerto Rico, and Mexico.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';line-height:1.28;margin-bottom:8pt;visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Forward-Looking Statements</font></p><p style="font-family:'Calibri','Helvetica','sans-serif';font-size:11pt;line-height:1.19;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';">The Company claims style="display:inline-block;min-width:21.6pt;text-indent:0pt;white-space:nowrap;">&#9679;</font><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Announced Executive Leadership Succession Plan</font></div><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><b style="font-weight:bold;">Springfield, MO, July 26, 2023</b><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> &#8211; </font>O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;O&#8217;Reilly&#8221;) (<font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Nasdaq: &#160;</font>ORLY), a leading retailer in the automotive aftermarket industry, today announced record revenue and earnings for its second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">nd</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Greg Johnson, O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s CEO, commented, &#8220;We are very pleased to report another quarter of continued strong growth, highlighted by a 9.0% increase in comparable store sales and a 16% increase in diluted earnings per share to $10.22. &#160;Team O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s commitment to providing consistently excellent customer service drove robust double-digit professional and solid DIY comparable store sales growth in the quarter. &#160;I want to congratulate our over 88,000 dedicated Team Members on their incredible performance in the second quarter and express my sincere appreciation for their relentless focus on delivering industry-leading service to our customers each and every day.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023, increased $398 million, or 11%, to $4.07 billion from $3.67 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the second quarter increased 11% to $2.09 billion (or 51.3% of sales) from $1.88 billion (or 51.3% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Selling, general and administrative expenses (&#8220;SG&amp;A&#8221;) for the second quarter increased 14% to $1.23 billion (or 30.3% of sales) from $1.09 billion (or 29.6% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for the second quarter increased 7% to $854 million (or 21.0% of sales) from $799 million (or 21.8% of sales) for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023, increased $51 million, or 9%, to $627 million (or 15.4% of sales) from $577 million (or 15.7% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the second quarter increased 16% to $10.22 on 61 million shares versus $8.78 on 66 million shares for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Year-to-Date Financial Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Johnson continued, &#8220;We have opened 100 net, new stores across 34 U.S. states, Puerto Rico, and Mexico so far in 2023 and are on pace to meet our goal of 180 to 190 net, new store openings in 2023. &#160;We continue to be very pleased with our new store performance, driven by our well-trained and technically-proficient Professional Parts People. &#160;We are also excited to celebrate the expansion of our distribution network with the opening of our first O&#8217;Reilly distribution center in Mexico in July. &#160;This new, 370,000 square foot facility strengthens our existing store network with enhanced inventory availability, empowering higher service levels and establishing the critical foundation for long-term store growth in Mexico.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Sales for the first six months of 2023 increased $810 million, or 12%, to $7.78 billion from $6.97 billion for the same period one year ago. &#160;Gross profit for the first six months of 2023 increased 11% to $3.98 billion (or 51.1% of sales) from $3.59 billion (or 51.6% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;SG&amp;A for the first six months of 2023 increased 13% to $2.41 billion (or 30.9% of sales) from $2.12 billion (or 30.5% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Operating income for </p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="background-color:#000000;clear:both;color:#000000;height:2pt;line-height:0;margin-bottom:30pt;margin-left:5.88%;margin-right:5.88%;margin-top:30pt;page-break-after:always;width:88.24%;border-width:0;"><div style="max-width:100%;padding-left:5.88%;padding-right:5.88%;position:relative;"><div style="clear:both;max-width:100%;position:relative;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">the first six months of 2023 increased 7% to $1.57 billion (or 20.2% of sales) from $1.47 billion (or 21.1% of sales) for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Net income for the first six months of 2023 increased $86 million, or 8%, to $1.14 billion (or 14.7% of sales) from $1.06 billion (or 15.2% of sales) for the same period one year ago. &#160;Diluted earnings per common share for the first six months of 2023 increased 16% to $18.49 on 62 million shares versus $15.94 on 66 million shares for the same period one year ago.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Mr. Johnson concluded, &#8220;The strong top-line performance we delivered through the first half of the year exceeded our expectations, and we remain pleased with our performance thus far in July. &#160;We believe the core underlying demand drivers of our industry remain solid, and more importantly, we remain confident in our Team&#8217;s ability to consistently execute our proven dual market strategy and expand our market share. &#160;Based on our strong year-to-date results and continued robust sales trends, we are increasing our full-year comparable store sales guidance from a range of 4% to 6% to a range of 5% to 7%. &#160;Finally, I would like to again thank Team O&#8217;Reilly for delivering strong results in the first half of 2023 &#8211; your commitment to our customers remains the key to O&#8217;Reilly&#8217;s ongoing success.&#8221;</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">2</font><sup style="font-size:8.25pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;vertical-align:top;">nd</sup><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;"> Quarter Comparable Store Sales Results</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">Comparable store sales are calculated based on the change in sales for U.S. stores open at least one year and exclude sales of specialty machinery, sales to independent parts stores, and sales to Team Members. &#160;Online sales for ship-to-home orders and pick-up-in-store orders for U.S. stores open at least one year are included in the comparable store sales calculation. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 9.0% for the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023, on top of 4.3% for the same period one year ago. &#160;Comparable store sales increased 9.8% for the six months ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023, on top of 4.5% for the same period one year ago. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Share Repurchase Program</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">During the second quarter ended June&#160;30,&#160;2023, the Company repurchased 0.8 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $904.37, for a total investment of $680 million. &#160;During the first six months of 2023, the Company repurchased 2.1 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $849.48, for a total investment of $1.79 billion. &#160;Excise tax on shares repurchased, assessed at one percent of the fair market value of net shares repurchased, was $16.5 million for the first six months of 2023. &#160;Subsequent to the end of the second quarter and through the date of this release, the Company repurchased an additional 0.1 million shares of its common stock, at an average price per share of $952.24, for a total investment of $119 million. &#160;The Company has repurchased a total of 92.7 million shares of its common stock under its share repurchase program since the inception of the program in January of 2011 and through the date of this release, at an average price of $236.52, for a total aggregate investment of $21.94 billion. &#160;As of the date of this release, the Company had approximately $1.81 billion remaining under its current share repurchase authorization. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:center;margin:24pt 0pt 0pt 0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p></div></div><hr style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;">The table below outlines the Company&#8217;s updated guidance for selected full-year 2023 financial data:</p><div align="left"><table style="border-collapse:collapse;font-size:16pt;height:max-content;padding-left:0pt;padding-right:0pt;width:100%;"><tr style="height:1pt;"><td style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">This release contains certain financial information not derived in accordance with United States generally accepted accounting principles (&#8220;GAAP&#8221;). &#160;These items include adjusted debt to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, amortization, share-based compensation, and rent (&#8220;EBITDAR&#8221;) and free cash flow. &#160;The Company does not, nor does it suggest investors should, consider such non-GAAP financial measures in isolation from, or as a substitute for, GAAP financial information. &#160;The Company believes that the presentation of adjusted debt to EBITDAR and free cash flow provide meaningful supplemental information to both management and investors that is indicative of the Company&#8217;s core operations. &#160;The Company has included a reconciliation of this additional information to the most comparable GAAP measure in the table above and the selected financial information below. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Executive Leadership Succession Plan</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;">Today, in a separate press release, O&#8217;Reilly also announced the Company&#8217;s leadership succession plan. &#160;Effective January 31, 2024, Greg Johnson, who currently serves as the Company&#8217;s Chief Executive Officer (&#8220;CEO&#8221;) will retire and, at that time, Brad Beckham, who currently serves as the Company&#8217;s Co-President, will be promoted to CEO, and Brent Kirby, who currently serves as the Company&#8217;s Co-President, will be promoted to President.</p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;"><font style="visibility:hidden;">&#8203;</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">Earnings Conference Call Information</font></p><p discuss its results as well as future expectations. &#160;Investors may listen to the conference call live on the Company&#8217;s website at <u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u> by clicking on &#8220;Investor Relations&#8221; and then &#8220;News Room.&#8221; &#160;Interested analysts are invited to join the call. &#160;The dial-in number for the call is (888) 506-0062 and the conference call identification number is 273805. &#160;A replay of the conference call will be available on the Company&#8217;s website through Friday, July 26, 2024. </p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt 0pt 3pt 0pt;"><font style="font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">About O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc.</font></p><p style="font-family:'Times New Roman','Times','serif';font-size:11pt;text-align:justify;margin:0pt;">O&#8217;Reilly Automotive, Inc. was founded in 1957 by the O&#8217;Reilly family and is one of the largest specialty retailers of automotive aftermarket parts, tools, supplies, equipment, and accessories in the United States, serving both the do-it-yourself and professional service provider markets. &#160;Visit the Company&#8217;s website at <u style="text-decoration-color:#000000;text-decoration-line:underline;text-decoration-style:solid;">www.OReillyAuto.com</u> for additional information about O&#8217;Reilly, including access to online shopping and current promotions, store locations, hours and services, </p></div><div style="clear:both;margin-bottom:30pt;width:100%;"><p
